setmetatable({},{['__\99\97\108\108']=function(e,h,d,t,n)if n then return e[n]elseif t then return e else e[h]=d end end})end until true;else do return setmetatable({},{['__\99\97\108\108']=function(e,d,t,h,n)if n then return e[n]elseif h then return e else e[d]=t end end})end end else do return d[t]end;end end end end),...)
